<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>This score can be performed either by solo harpsichord or a small ensemble. If by an ensemble, the top line would be played by one or more treble instruments including flute, recorder, violin and oboe; cello, viola da gamba, or other bass instrument would play the bass line; and harpsichord would play both the bass line and realized harmonies based on the figures.
</td></tr>

<div class="we_file_download plainlinks">

<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Concerts Royaux
</td></tr>

</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>

<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="fr">Concerts royaux (françois couperin)</span>; <span title="fr">Concerts Royaux (François Couperin)</span>; <span title="fr">Concerts royaux (Francois Couperin)</span>; <span title="it">Concerti reali</span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IFC 4
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 suites "concerts"
<dl><dt><ul><li>Premier Concert
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Prélude
</dd><dd>2. Allemande
</dd><dd>3. Sarabande
</dd><dd>4. Gavotte
</dd><dd>5. Gigue
</dd><dd>6. Menuet en Trio
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Second Concert
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Prélude
</dd><dd>2. Allemande Fuguée
</dd><dd>3. Air Tendre
</dd><dd>4. Air Contrefugué
</dd><dd>5. Échos
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Troisième Concert
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Prélude
</dd><dd>2. Allemande
</dd><dd>3. Courante
</dd><dd>4. Sarabande
</dd><dd>5. Gavotte
</dd><dd>6. Muzette
</dd><dd>6a. Muzette
</dd><dd>7. Chaconne
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Quatrième Concert
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Prélude
</dd><dd>2. Allemande
</dd><dd>3. Courante Françoise
</dd><dd>4. Courante à l’italiéne
</dd><dd>5. Sarabande
</dd><dd>6. Rigaudon
</dd><dd>7. Forlane
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1722
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>Harpsichord (solo), or 2-3 treble instruments (flute, violin, oboe) with continuo
</td></tr></table>
